Use when writing, refactoring, or reviewing TypeScript/TSX, designing types/APIs, or resolving type errors.\n---\n\n# TypeScript Conventions (Pragmatic)\n\n## Goal\nWrite TypeScript that is **readable, safe, maintainable, and testable**, while matching the repo's existing style and constraints.\n\n## Common conventions (non-prescriptive)\n\nUse these as defaults when they fit; follow the repo when they don't.\n\n- **Consistency first**: mirror nearby patterns, naming, exports, and tooling (lint/format).\n- **Clarity at boundaries**: be explicit where data crosses a boundary (exports, I/O, env, API calls).\n- **Simple, communicative types**: model the domain clearly; prefer readability over clever types.\n- **Type safety without drama**: avoid unsafe assertions; when input is untrusted, use `unknown` and narrow/validate.\n- **Intentional errors**: throw `Error` objects, add helpful context, and avoid silently swallowing failures.\n- **Testable design**: keep core logic deterministic; isolate side effects; inject dependencies rather than hard-coding globals.\n\n## Type modeling (quick notes)\n\n- Teams often use **unions / discriminated unions** for domain states, and handle cases exhaustively when it improves correctness.\n- For constants/lookup tables, teams often use **`as const`** to preserve literal types.\n- Prefer immutability/pure logic when it makes reasoning easier; don't force it if it reduces clarity.\n" }

The approved PayPal order id is appended by PayPal\n * as a `token` query parameter.\n */\n returnUrl: string;\n /**\n * @description\n * The URL on the storefront to which PayPal redirects the buyer if they\n * cancel the approval flow.\n */\n cancelUrl: string;\n /**\n * @description\n * Optional brand name shown to the buyer on the PayPal approval pages.\n */\n brandName?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * @description\n * The result of creating a PayPal order, returned to the storefront so it can\n * redirect the buyer to PayPal for approval.\n */\nexport interface CreatePayPalOrderResult {\n /** The PayPal-generated order id. */\n paypalOrderId: string;\n /** The current PayPal order status (e.g. `CREATED`). */\n status: string;\n /** The URL to which the buyer must be redirected to approve the payment. */\n approvalUrl: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * @description\n * The result of capturing an approved PayPal order.\n */\nexport interface CapturePayPalOrderResult {\n /** The PayPal-generated order id that was captured. */\n paypalOrderId: string;\n /** The order-level status after capture (`COMPLETED` on success). */\n orderStatus: string;\n /** The PayPal capture id, used for later refund operations. */\n captureId: string;\n /** The status of the individual capture (`COMPLETED` on success). */\n captureStatus: string;\n /** The captured currency code, as reported by PayPal. */\n currencyCode?: string;\n /** The captured amount as a decimal string, as reported by PayPal. */\n value?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * @description\n * The shape of the `metadata` passed by the storefront to the\n * `addPaymentToOrder` mutation when paying with PayPal.\n */\nexport interface PayPalPaymentMetadata {\n /** The PayPal order id obtained from the `createPayPalOrder` mutation. */\n paypalOrderId?: string;\n}\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "content": "import { Inject, Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';\nimport { Logger } from '@vendure/core';\nimport {\n ApiError,\n CheckoutPaymentIntent,\n Client,\n CustomError,\n Environment,\n LogLevel,\n Order as PayPalOrder,\n OrdersController,\n} from '@paypal/paypal-server-sdk';\n\nimport { loggerCtx, PAYPAL_PLUGIN_OPTIONS } from './constants';\nimport { CapturePayPalOrderResult, CreatePayPalOrderResult, PayPalPluginOptions } from './types';\n\n/**\n * @description\n * Wraps the PayPal Server SDK and exposes the order operations required by the\n * plugin. The SDK client is constructed once and reused; OAuth2 access tokens\n * are managed and refreshed internally by the SDK.\n *\n * All credentials are sourced from the injected {@link PayPalPluginOptions} and\n * are never logged.\n */\n@Injectable()\nexport class PayPalService {\n private readonly ordersController: OrdersController;\n\n constructor(@Inject(PAYPAL_PLUGIN_OPTIONS) private readonly options: PayPalPluginOptions) {\n const client = new Client({\n clientCredentialsAuthCredentials: {\n oAuthClientId: options.clientId,\n oAuthClientSecret: options.clientSecret,\n },\n timeout: 0,\n environment:\n options.environment === 'production' ? Environment.Production : Environment.Sandbox,\n logging: {\n logLevel: LogLevel.Info,\n // Never log request/response bodies, which can contain sensitive data.\n logRequest: { logBody: false },\n logResponse: { logHeaders: false },\n },\n });\n this.ordersController = new OrdersController(client);\n }\n\n /**\n * @description\n * Creates a PayPal order with `CAPTURE` intent for the given amount and\n * returns the order id and the buyer approval URL.\n *\n * @param amountMinorUnits The amount in integer minor units (e.g. `1000` = $10.00).\n * @param currencyCode The three-character ISO-4217 currency code.\n * @param referenceId An opaque reference (the Vendure order code) attached to\n * the PayPal order for reconciliation.\n */\n async createOrder(\n amountMinorUnits: number,\n currencyCode: string,\n referenceId: string,\n ): Promise<CreatePayPalOrderResult> {\n let result: PayPalOrder;\n try {\n const response = await this.ordersController.createOrder({\n body: {\n intent: CheckoutPaymentIntent.Capture,\n purchaseUnits: [\n {\n referenceId,\n amount: {\n currencyCode,\n value: this.toPayPalValue(amountMinorUnits, currencyCode),\n },\n },\n ],\n paymentSource: {\n paypal: {\n experienceContext: {\n returnUrl: this.options.returnUrl,\n cancelUrl: this.options.cancelUrl,\n ...(this.options.brandName\n ? { brandName: this.options.brandName }\n : {}),\n },\n },\n },\n },\n prefer: 'return=representation',\n });\n result = response.result;\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('create the PayPal order', e);\n }\n\n if (!result?.id) {\n throw new Error('PayPal did not return an order id when creating the order');\n }\n\n const approvalUrl = this.extractApprovalUrl(result);\n if (!approvalUrl) {\n throw new Error('PayPal did not return a buyer approval URL for the created order');\n }\n\n return {\n paypalOrderId: result.id,\n status: result.status ?? 'CREATED',\n approvalUrl,\n };\n }\n\n /**\n * @description\n * Captures payment for a PayPal order that the buyer has already approved.\n * Returns the capture id and status used to settle the Vendure payment and\n * to support later refunds.\n *\n * @param paypalOrderId The PayPal order id returned by {@link createOrder}.\n */\n async captureOrder(paypalOrderId: string): Promise<CapturePayPalOrderResult> {\n let result: PayPalOrder;\n try {\n const response = await this.ordersController.captureOrder({\n id: paypalOrderId,\n prefer: 'return=representation',\n });\n result = response.result;\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('capture the PayPal order', e);\n }\n\n const capture = result?.purchaseUnits?.[0]?.payments?.captures?.[0];\n if (!result?.id || !capture?.id || !capture.status) {\n throw new Error('PayPal capture response did not contain a completed capture');\n }\n\n return {\n paypalOrderId: result.id,\n orderStatus: result.status ?? 'UNKNOWN',\n captureId: capture.id,\n captureStatus: capture.status,\n currencyCode: capture.amount?.currencyCode,\n value: capture.amount?.value,\n };\n }\n\n /**\n * Converts an integer amount in minor units into the decimal string format\n * expected by PayPal, honouring the number of fraction digits defined for\n * the currency (e.g. 2 for USD, 0 for JPY).\n */\n private toPayPalValue(amountMinorUnits: number, currencyCode: string): string {\n const fractionDigits = this.getCurrencyFractionDigits(currencyCode);\n const divisor = Math.pow(10, fractionDigits);\n return (amountMinorUnits / divisor).toFixed(fractionDigits);\n }\n\n private getCurrencyFractionDigits(currencyCode: string): number {\n try {\n const format = new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {\n style: 'currency',\n currency: currencyCode,\n });\n return format.resolvedOptions().maximumFractionDigits ?? 2;\n } catch {\n return 2;\n }\n }\n\n private extractApprovalUrl(order: PayPalOrder): string | undefined {\n const link = order.links?.find(l => l.rel === 'approve' || l.rel === 'payer-action');\n return link?.href;\n }\n\n /**\n * Normalises any thrown SDK value into a single `Error` with a safe,\n * descriptive message, while logging the structured PayPal error detail.\n * Credentials are never included in the message or the log.\n */\n private toError(action: string, e: unknown): Error {\n if (e instanceof ApiError) {\n const detail = e instanceof CustomError ? safeStringify(e.result) : e.message;\n Logger.error(\n `Failed to ${action} (status ${e.statusCode}): ${detail}`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n return new Error(`Failed to ${action}: PayPal returned status ${e.statusCode}`);\n }\n const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);\n Logger.error(`Failed to ${action}: ${message}`, loggerCtx);\n return new Error(`Failed to ${action}: ${message}`);\n }\n}\n\nfunction safeStringify(value: unknown): string {\n try {\n return JSON.stringify(value);\n } catch {\n return String(value);\n }\n}\n" }

e.message : String(e);\n return {\n amount,\n state: 'Declined' as const,\n errorMessage,\n metadata: {\n public: { errorMessage },\n },\n };\n }\n },\n\n settlePayment: async (): Promise<SettlePaymentResult> => {\n // The payment is captured immediately in `createPayment`, so there is\n // nothing further to do here for the immediate-capture flow.\n return { success: true };\n },\n});\n" }

Minor-unit→decimal conversion honours currency precision (USD→2dp, JPY→0dp). Errors normalized & logged without leaking credentials. | | `paypal-payment-handler.ts` | `PaymentMethodHandler` (code `paypal`): `createPayment` captures the approved order → `Settled`/`Declined`; `settlePayment` returns success (already captured). | | `api/paypal-shop.resolver.ts` + `api-extensions.ts` | Shop API mutation `createPayPalOrder` → `{ paypalOrderId, status, approvalUrl }` for the active order. | | `paypal.plugin.ts` | Wires handler + Shop API; auto-creates the `paypal` PaymentMethod on bootstrap (no manual Admin setup needed). Shop API: **`POST http://localhost:3000/shop-api`** (body type **GraphQL** or JSON `{ "query": "...", "variables": {...} }`). > **Session handling:** On the *first* request, copy the `vendure-auth-token` response **header** and send it as `Authorization: Bearer <token>` on every subsequent request — this keeps the same active order. **Step 1 — Add an item to the cart** ```graphql mutation { addItemToOrder(productVariantId: "1", quantity: 1) { ... on Order { id code totalWithTax currencyCode } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` → Capture the `vendure-auth-token` header now. **Step 2 — Create the PayPal order** ```graphql mutation { createPayPalOrder { paypalOrderId status approvalUrl } } ``` ✅ Expected: `status: "CREATED"`, a `paypalOrderId` (e.g. `5O190127TN364715T`), and an `approvalUrl` (`https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/checkoutnow?token=...`). **Step 3 — Approve as the buyer (browser)** Open the `approvalUrl` in a browser, log in with your **PayPal sandbox buyer** account, and approve. PayPal redirects to your `returnUrl`. Keep the `paypalOrderId` from Step 2. **Step 4 — Bring the order to ArrangingPayment** (run these with the same Bearer token) ```graphql mutation { setCustomerForOrder(input:{ emailAddress:"test@buyer.com", firstName:"Test", lastName:"Buyer" }) { ... on Order { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { setOrderShippingAddress(input:{ fullName:"Test Buyer", streetLine1:"1 Test St", city:"London", postalCode:"SW1", countryCode:"GB" }) { ... on Order { id } } } mutation { setOrderShippingMethod(shippingMethodId:"1") { ... on Order { id shippingWithTax totalWithTax } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { transitionOrderToState(state:"ArrangingPayment") { ... on Order { id state } ... on OrderStateTransitionError { message } } } ``` **Step 5 — Add payment (this triggers the capture)** ```graphql mutation { addPaymentToOrder(input:{ method:"paypal", metadata:{ paypalOrderId:"<paypalOrderId from Step 2>" } }) { ... on Order { id state payments { id amount state transactionId metadata } } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } ... on PaymentFailedError { paymentErrorMessage } } } ``` ✅ **Expected success response:** order `state: "PaymentSettled"`, with a payment `state: "Settled"`, a `transactionId` (the PayPal capture id), and `metadata` containing `paypalOrderId`, `captureId`, `captureStatus: "COMPLETED"`. ❌ If the buyer didn't approve, or `paypalOrderId` is wrong/already captured, you'll get `PaymentFailedError` with `paymentErrorMessage` describing the PayPal failure — and the order stays in `ArrangingPayment`. --- ⏸️ **Stopping here per the usecase-by-usecase protocol.** I will not touch any code for UC2 until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** When you've run the Postman flow, tell me whether the capture succeeded — I'll then record the `first_call_made` milestone and we can proceed. --- ## References ### Endpoints - I have the full UC2 contract: - `OrdersController.authorizeOrder({id})` → authorization at `result.purchaseUnits[0].payments.authorizations[0]` (`.id`, `.status`, `.amount`). - `PaymentsController.captureAuthorizedPayment({authorizationId, body:{finalCapture}})` → `CapturedPayment` (`.id`, `.status`, `.amount`). **Design (extends UC1 without breaking it):** the order's intent is chosen at `createPayPalOrder` time (new optional `intent` arg, defaults to `CAPTURE` → UC1 unchanged). The single `paypal` handler gains an `intent` config arg: `capture` (UC1 — createPayment captures, settle is a no-op) vs `authorize` (UC2 — createPayment authorizes → `Authorized`; settlePayment captures the authorization). capture the `vendure-auth-token` response header and send it as `Authorization: Bearer <token>` on all later Shop API calls. ```graphql mutation { addItemToOrder(productVariantId: "1", quantity: 1) { ... on Order { id code totalWithTax } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } ``` **Step 2 — Create an AUTHORIZE-intent PayPal order** ```graphql mutation { createPayPalOrder(intent: AUTHORIZE) { paypalOrderId status approvalUrl } } ``` ✅ Expected: `status: "CREATED"` + `paypalOrderId` + `approvalUrl`. **Step 3 — Approve in the browser** as your PayPal **sandbox buyer** (open `approvalUrl`). Keep the `paypalOrderId`. **Step 4 — Bring the order to ArrangingPayment** (Shop API, same Bearer token) ```graphql mutation { setCustomerForOrder(input:{ emailAddress:"test@buyer.com", firstName:"Test", lastName:"Buyer" }) { ... on Order { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { setOrderShippingAddress(input:{ fullName:"Test Buyer", streetLine1:"1 Test St", city:"London", postalCode:"SW1", countryCode:"GB" }) { ... on Order { id } } } mutation { setOrderShippingMethod(shippingMethodId:"1") { ... on Order { id totalWithTax } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { transitionOrderToState(state:"ArrangingPayment") { ... on Order { id state } ... on OrderStateTransitionError { message } } } ``` **Step 5 — Authorize the payment (reserves funds, no capture yet)** ```graphql mutation { addPaymentToOrder(input:{ method:"paypal-authorize", metadata:{ paypalOrderId:"<paypalOrderId>" } }) { ... on Order { id state payments { id state transactionId metadata } } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } ... on PaymentFailedError { paymentErrorMessage } } } ``` ✅ Expected: order `state: "PaymentAuthorized"`; payment `state: "Authorized"`, `transactionId` = the **authorization id**, `metadata.authorizationStatus: "CREATED"`. **No money has moved yet.** In the PayPal sandbox dashboard the transaction shows as **Pending/Authorized**, not Completed. **Note the payment `id`** from the response for Step 7. **Step 6 — Authenticate to the Admin API** (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`); capture *its* `vendure-auth-token` header → Bearer for the Admin call. ```graphql mutation { login(username:"superadmin", password:"superadmin") { ... on CurrentUser { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } ``` **Step 7 — Capture the authorized funds (Admin API)** — this is the "before shipment" capture: ```graphql mutation { settlePayment(id: "<payment id from Step 5>") { ... on Payment { id state transactionId metadata } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } ... on SettlePaymentError { paymentErrorMessage } } } ``` ✅ Expected: payment `state: "Settled"`, `metadata.captureId` populated, `metadata.captureStatus: "COMPLETED"`. The order moves to **`PaymentSettled`**, and the PayPal sandbox dashboard now shows the transaction as **Completed/Captured**. ❌ Failure cases: an unapproved/expired authorization or wrong id returns `SettlePaymentError` with `paymentErrorMessage`, and the payment stays `Authorized`. --- ⏸️ **Stopping here per the usecase-by-usecase protocol.** I won't touch any code for UC3 (Payment Cancellation / Void) until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** --- ## References ### Endpoints - 🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "old_string": " * @param authorizationId The PayPal authorization id from {@link authorizeOrder}.\n */\n async captureAuthorization(authorizationId: string): Promise<CaptureAuthorizationResult> {\n let capture: CapturedPayment;\n try {\n const response = await this.paymentsController.captureAuthorizedPayment({\n authorizationId,\n prefer: 'return=representation',\n body: { finalCapture: true },\n });\n capture = response.result;\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('capture the authorized PayPal payment', e);\n }\n\n if (!capture?.id || !capture.status) {\n throw new Error('PayPal capture-authorization response did not contain a capture');\n }\n\n return {\n captureId: capture.id,\n captureStatus: capture.status,\n currencyCode: capture.amount?.currencyCode,\n value: capture.amount?.value,\n };\n }", "new_string": " * @param authorizationId The PayPal authorization id from {@link authorizeOrder}.\n * @param paypalOrderId The originating PayPal order id, used to recover the\n * capture details if a previous attempt already captured the funds.\n */\n async captureAuthorization(\n authorizationId: string,\n paypalOrderId?: string,\n ): Promise<CaptureAuthorizationResult> {\n try {\n return await this.withRetry(\n 'capture the authorized PayPal payment',\n async attempt => {\n // `captureAuthorizedPayment` does not accept an idempotency key,\n // so before retrying we check whether a previous (possibly\n // timed-out) attempt already captured the funds. Returns `undefined`\n * if the authorization has not been captured or the lookup is inconclusive.\n */\n private async findExistingCapture(\n authorizationId: string,\n paypalOrderId?: string,\n ): Promise<CaptureAuthorizationResult | undefined> {\n let status: string | undefined;\n try {\n const response = await this.paymentsController.getAuthorizedPayment({ authorizationId });\n status = response.result?.status;\n } catch {\n // If we cannot determine the status, let the caller proceed/fail normally.\n return undefined;\n }\n if (status !== 'CAPTURED' && status !== 'PARTIALLY_CAPTURED') {\n return undefined;\n }\n\n // The funds are already captured. Recover the real capture id from the\n // PayPal order so refunds (Use Cases 4 & 5) can reference it.\n if (paypalOrderId) {\n try {\n const order = await this.ordersController.getOrder({ id: paypalOrderId });\n const capture = order.result?.purchaseUnits?.[0]?.payments?.captures?.[0];\n if (capture?.id && capture.status) {\n Logger.warn(\n `Recovered existing capture ${capture.id} for authorization ${authorizationId}`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n return {\n captureId: capture.id,\n captureStatus: capture.status,\n currencyCode: capture.amount?.currencyCode,\n value: capture.amount?.value,\n };\n }\n } catch {\n // Fall through to the warning below.\n }\n }\n\n Logger.warn(\n `Authorization ${authorizationId} is already captured but the capture id could not ` +\n 'be recovered; manual reconciliation may be required',\n loggerCtx,\n );\n return { captureId: authorizationId, captureStatus: 'COMPLETED' };\n }" }

🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "old_string": " private extractApprovalUrl(order: PayPalOrder): string | undefined {\n const link = order.links?.find(l => l.rel === 'approve' || l.rel === 'payer-action');\n return link?.href;\n }", "new_string": " private extractApprovalUrl(order: PayPalOrder): string | undefined {\n const link = order.links?.find(l => l.rel === 'approve' || l.rel === 'payer-action');\n return link?.href;\n }\n\n /**\n * Runs the given operation, retrying with exponential backoff when it fails\n * with a transient error (network timeout/reset, HTTP 429 or 5xx). The\n * callback receives the 1-based attempt number so it can apply idempotency\n * safeguards on retries.\n */\n private async withRetry<T>(\n action: string,\n fn: (attempt: number) => Promise<T>,\n ): Promise<T> {\n let lastError: unknown;\n for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= MAX_ATTEMPTS; attempt++) {\n try {\n return await fn(attempt);\n } catch (e) {\n lastError = e;\n if (attempt < MAX_ATTEMPTS && this.isTransient(e)) {\n const delayMs = RETRY_BASE_DELAY_MS * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1);\n Logger.warn(\n `Transient error while attempting to ${action} ` +\n `(attempt ${attempt}/${MAX_ATTEMPTS}); retrying in ${delayMs}ms`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n await sleep(delayMs);\n continue;\n }\n throw e;\n }\n }\n throw lastError;\n }\n\n /** Determines whether an error is worth retrying. */\n private isTransient(e: unknown): boolean {\n if (e instanceof ApiError) {\n const status = e.statusCode;\n return status === 429 || (typeof status === 'number' && status >= 500);\n }\n const code = (e as { code?: unknown })?.code;\n const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : '';\n return TRANSIENT_NETWORK_CODES.some(c => code === c || message.includes(c));\n }\n\n /** Detects the PayPal \"authorization already captured\" business error. */\n private isAlreadyCaptured(e: unknown): boolean {\n if (!(e instanceof ApiError) || e.statusCode !== 422) {\n return false;\n }\n const detail = e instanceof CustomError ? safeStringify(e.result) : safeStringify(e.body);\n return detail.includes('AUTHORIZATION_ALREADY_CAPTURED');\n }" }

🤖 Claude
## ✅ Fixed — root cause and resolution **What happened:** Your first `settlePayment` hit a transient `connect ETIMEDOUT` (a network blip to PayPal's edge, before PayPal processed the capture). My handler treated that as a hard failure and returned `success: false`, which transitioned the Payment `Authorized → Error`. When you retried, that second call genuinely captured on PayPal (HTTP 201, capture `15D11495FR379320A`) — but Vendure can't legally go `Error → Settled`, hence `PAYMENT_STATE_TRANSITION_ERROR`. So one transient blip permanently wedged the payment. **The fix (in `paypal.service.ts`):** 1. **Retry-with-backoff on transient errors** — every PayPal call now retries (up to 3 attempts, exponential backoff) on network errors (`ETIMEDOUT`, `ECONNRESET`, …) and HTTP 429/5xx. Your exact case (timeout *before* capture) now simply retries inside the same `settlePayment` call and settles cleanly — the payment never drops to `Error`. Non-transient 4xx errors are **not** retried. 2. **Idempotency keys** (`paypalRequestId`) on `captureOrder` (UC1) and `authorizeOrder` (UC2) — the MCP confirmed these support it (6h retention), so retries can't duplicate a charge/authorization. 3. **Double-capture guard for `captureAuthorizedPayment`** — the MCP confirmed this endpoint has *no* idempotency-key param. So before any retry, I call `getAuthorizedPayment`; if it already shows `CAPTURED`, I recover the real capture id from `getOrder(paypalOrderId)` and return that instead of capturing again. This is exactly the scenario that would have double-charged a buyer (timeout *after* a successful capture). **Self-test:** 20/20 unit tests pass (added: transient-retry-then-succeed, no-double-capture recovery, no-retry-on-non-transient, createOrder retry, plus idempotency-key assertions). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged. **About the currently-stuck payment** (order in `Error`, but PayPal capture `15D11495FR379320A` succeeded): the code fix prevents recurrences but can't un-wedge an already-`Error` payment (`Error → Settled` is disallowed by Vendure's default payment state machine — intentionally, so I won't weaken it). For sandbox testing just run a **fresh** UC2 order to verify the fix. The orphaned sandbox capture can be refunded from the PayPal sandbox dashboard or ignored. --- ## 🧪 Re-verify UC2 (after restarting the dev server) Run the same UC2 Postman flow from before (add item → `createPayPalOrder(intent: AUTHORIZE)` → approve in browser → setCustomer/shipping/transition → `addPaymentToOrder(method:"paypal-authorize", metadata:{paypalOrderId})` → Admin `login` → `settlePayment(id)`). ✅ Expected now: even if a transient timeout occurs, `settlePayment` returns payment `state: "Settled"` with `metadata.captureId` + `captureStatus: "COMPLETED"`, and the order reaches `PaymentSettled` — no `PAYMENT_STATE_TRANSITION_ERROR`. To deliberately exercise the retry, you can momentarily throttle your connection during the settle call; the server log will show `Transient error while attempting to capture the authorized PayPal payment (attempt 1/3); retrying…` followed by success. --- ⏸️ Still paused on the usecase protocol — I won't start UC3 until you confirm UC2 verifies and reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** --- ## References ### Endpoints - [CaptureAuthorizedPayment](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/api-endpoints/payments/capture-authorized-payment) - [GetCapturedPayment](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/api-endpoints/payments/get-captured-payment) - [GetAuthorizedPayment](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/api-endpoints/payments/get-authorized-payment) - [CaptureOrder](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/api-endpoints/orders/capture-order) - [AuthorizeOrder](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/api-endpoints/orders/authorize-order) ### Models - [CaptureRequest](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/capture-request) - [CapturedPayment](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/captured-payment) - [PaymentAuthorization](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/payment-authorization) - [OrderCaptureRequest](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/order-capture-request) - [Order](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/order) - [OrderAuthorizeRequest](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/order-authorize-request) - [OrderAuthorizeResponse](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/models/structures/order-authorize-response) ### Getting Started - [Getting Started](https://www.paypalobjects.com/serversdk/typescript/getting-started#environments)

UC4 is complete and self-tested. ## ✅ Usecase 4 (Full Refund) is implemented and self-tested. **What was added** (additive; UC1–UC3 untouched): | File | Change | |------|--------| | `paypal.service.ts` | New `refundCapture(captureId, options?)` → `PaymentsController.refundCapturedPayment`. **Omits the body for a full refund** (per the PayPal contract); accepts an optional amount for partial refunds (wired up in UC5). Uses `return=representation`, an amount-specific `paypalRequestId` idempotency key, and the transient-retry wrapper. | | `paypal-payment-handler.ts` | New `createRefund` lifecycle method: reads `captureId` from `payment.metadata`, performs a **full** refund, and maps the PayPal refund status to Vendure's `RefundState` (`COMPLETED→Settled`, `PENDING→Pending`, else `Failed`). Partial-amount requests return `Failed` for now (explicitly scoped to UC5) so a partial refund can never silently over-refund. | | `types.ts` | New `RefundCaptureResult`. | **Self-test:** 27/27 unit tests pass (4 new: full-refund no-body + `…-full` key, partial sends amount + amount-keyed id, no-refund-in-response throws, error wrapping). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged. --- ## 🧪 Manual verification via Postman First produce a **settled** payment (UC1 immediate-capture is the quickest), then refund it. **Steps 1–5 — get a settled payment** (Shop API; capture `vendure-auth-token` after step 1 and send as Bearer): ```graphql mutation { addItemToOrder(productVariantId:"1", quantity:1){ ... on Order { id code totalWithTax } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { createPayPalOrder { paypalOrderId status approvalUrl } } # CAPTURE intent (default) # → open approvalUrl in browser, approve as sandbox buyer mutation { setCustomerForOrder(input:{ emailAddress:"test@buyer.com", firstName:"Test", lastName:"Buyer" }){ ... on Order { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { setOrderShippingAddress(input:{ fullName:"Test Buyer", streetLine1:"1 Test St", city:"London", postalCode:"SW1", countryCode:"GB" }){ ... on Order { id } } } mutation { setOrderShippingMethod(shippingMethodId:"1"){ ... on Order { id totalWithTax } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } mutation { transitionOrderToState(state:"ArrangingPayment"){ ... on Order { id state } ... on OrderStateTransitionError { message } } } mutation { addPaymentToOrder(input:{ method:"paypal", metadata:{ paypalOrderId:"<paypalOrderId>" } }){ ... on Order { id state totalWithTax payments { id state transactionId metadata } } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` ✅ Order `PaymentSettled`. **Note the `payments[0].id`** and the order's **`totalWithTax`** (an integer in minor units, e.g. `129900`). **Step 6 — Admin login** (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`; capture its `vendure-auth-token` → Bearer): ```graphql mutation { login(username:"superadmin", password:"superadmin"){ ... on CurrentUser { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } ``` **Step 7 — Full refund (Admin API)** — set `amount` to the exact `totalWithTax` from Step 5: ```graphql mutation { refundOrder(input: { paymentId: "<payment id>", amount: <totalWithTax>, reason: "Customer return" }) { ... on Refund { id state total transactionId metadata } ... on RefundAmountError { errorCode message } ... on AlreadyRefundedError { errorCode message } ... on RefundOrderStateError { errorCode message } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` ✅ Expected: a `Refund` with `state: "Settled"`, `total` = the full amount, `transactionId` = the PayPal refund id, and `metadata.refundStatus: "COMPLETED"`. In the PayPal sandbox dashboard the original capture now shows **Refunded**. ❌ Re-running it returns `AlreadyRefundedError` (and even if Vendure did re-issue, the idempotency key makes PayPal return the original refund — no double refund). > Tip: passing an `amount` **less than** `totalWithTax` currently returns a `Refund` in `Failed` state with `metadata.errorMessage: "Partial refunds are not yet supported"` — that's the intentional UC4 boundary; partial refunds arrive in UC5. --- ⏸️ **Stopping per the usecase protocol.** I won't start UC5 (Partial Refund) until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** --- ## References ### Endpoints - 27/27 pass, type-check clean. UC5 is complete and self-tested. ## ✅ Usecase 5 (Partial Refund) is implemented and self-tested. **What changed:** | File | Change | |------|--------| | `paypal.service.ts` | `refundCapture(captureId, idempotencyKey, partial?)` — now takes the idempotency key from the caller. When `partial` is supplied it sends an `amount` body (partial refund); otherwise no body (full refund). | | `paypal-payment-handler.ts` | `createRefund` no longer rejects partial amounts. It sends a partial refund when `amount < payment.amount` (with `order.currencyCode`) and a full refund otherwise. | **The key correctness fix:** my UC4 idempotency key was amount-based (`refund-<capture>-<amount>`), which would have caused **two legitimate same-amount partial refunds to collide** — PayPal would dedupe the second and silently under-refund. The plan explicitly allows *multiple* partial refunds. I confirmed in `payment.service.ts` that the `payment.refunds` relation is loaded when the handler runs (and the new Refund isn't persisted yet), so the key is now `refund-<captureId>-<priorRefundCount>` — **stable across internal retries, unique across distinct refunds**. Each partial gets its own sequence number, so same-amount partials both go through; a retried single refund stays idempotent. **Self-test:** 27/27 unit tests pass (refund tests updated for the explicit-key signature, covering full no-body, partial-with-amount, key forwarding, no-refund, and error wrapping). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged. --- ## 🧪 Manual verification via Postman **Steps 1–5 — get a settled payment** (UC1 immediate-capture, exactly as in UC4): add item → `createPayPalOrder` → approve in browser → setCustomer/shipping/transition → `addPaymentToOrder(method:"paypal", metadata:{paypalOrderId})` → `PaymentSettled`. **Note the `payments[0].id` and `totalWithTax`.** **Step 6 — Admin login** (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`; capture its `vendure-auth-token` → Bearer). **Step 7 — First partial refund** — `amount` **less than** `totalWithTax` (e.g. if total is `129900`, refund `40000`): ```graphql mutation { refundOrder(input: { paymentId: "<payment id>", amount: 40000, reason: "Partial return - 1 item" }) { ... on Refund { id state total transactionId metadata } ... on RefundAmountError { errorCode message maximumRefundable } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` ✅ Expected: `Refund` with `state: "Settled"`, `total: 40000`, `transactionId` = PayPal refund id, `metadata.refundStatus: "COMPLETED"`. PayPal sandbox shows the capture **partially refunded**. **Step 8 — Second partial refund (same or different amount)** — proves multiple partials work and the idempotency-key fix: ```graphql mutation { refundOrder(input: { paymentId: "<payment id>", amount: 40000, reason: "Partial return - 2nd item" }) { ... on Refund { id state total transactionId metadata } ... on RefundAmountError { errorCode message maximumRefundable } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` ✅ Expected: a **distinct** `Refund` (new `id` and a new PayPal `transactionId`, not a duplicate of Step 7) — confirming same-amount partials are no longer deduped. **Step 9 — Over-refund guard** — request more than the remaining refundable amount: ```graphql mutation { refundOrder(input: { paymentId: "<payment id>", amount: 999999, reason: "Too much" }) { ... on Refund { id state total } ... on RefundAmountError { errorCode message maximumRefundable } } } ``` ✅ Expected: `RefundAmountError` with `maximumRefundable` = what's left (Vendure blocks it before calling PayPal). > Full refunds (UC4) still work unchanged: pass `amount` equal to `totalWithTax` → sent to PayPal with no amount body. --- ⏸️ **Stopping per the usecase protocol.** I won't start UC6 (Subscription Billing) until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** Heads up: UC6 is the largest — a separate NestJS module with TypeORM entities, resolvers, and the `Scheduler` — so it'll be a bigger change set than UC1–UC5. --- ## References ### Endpoints - 🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\subscription\\paypal-subscription.service.ts", "content": "import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';\nimport {\n CustomerService,\n ID,\n Logger,\n RequestContext,\n TransactionalConnection,\n} from '@vendure/core';\nimport { randomUUID } from 'crypto';\n\nimport { loggerCtx } from '../constants';\nimport { PayPalService } from '../paypal.service';\nimport { PayPalSubscription } from './paypal-subscription.entity';\nimport {\n CreateBillingPlanInput,\n CreateBillingPlanResult,\n PayPalSubscriptionStatus,\n TERMINAL_SUBSCRIPTION_STATUSES,\n} from './subscription-types';\n\nconst KNOWN_STATUSES: PayPalSubscriptionStatus[] = [\n 'APPROVAL_PENDING',\n 'APPROVED',\n 'ACTIVE',\n 'SUSPENDED',\n 'CANCELLED',\n 'EXPIRED',\n];\n\nfunction normalizeStatus(status: string): PayPalSubscriptionStatus {\n return (KNOWN_STATUSES as string[]).includes(status)\n ? 🤖 Claude
Baseline unchanged at 1138 (all pre-existing). UC6 is complete and self-tested. ## ✅ Usecase 6 (Subscription Billing) is implemented and self-tested. This is the large one — a self-contained subscription module inside the plugin, exactly as the architecture called for. **New module** (`example-plugins/paypal-plugin/subscription/`): | File | Responsibility | |------|----------------| | `paypal-subscription.entity.ts` | `PayPalSubscription` TypeORM entity (paypalSubscriptionId, planId, status, customerId, approvalUrl, lastSyncedAt) — registered via the plugin's `entities`. | | `subscription-types.ts` | Status union, interval types, plan/subscription input & result types. | | `paypal-subscription.service.ts` | Business layer: persists the local mirror, links to the Vendure customer, lists/filters, syncs status, cancel/suspend/activate, failed-payment retry. | | `api/subscription-api-extensions.ts` | Admin + Shop GraphQL SDL (shared `PayPalSubscription` type, `PayPalIntervalUnit` enum). | | `api/paypal-subscription-admin.resolver.ts` | Merchant ops (plan lifecycle + subscription management), gated by `ReadPaymentMethod`/`UpdatePaymentMethod`. | | `api/paypal-subscription-shop.resolver.ts` | Customer ops (subscribe, list own, cancel own — with ownership checks), gated by `Authenticated`. | | `paypal-subscription-sync.task.ts` | `ScheduledTask` (hourly) reconciling non-terminal subscription statuses with PayPal — registered via `config.schedulerOptions.tasks`. | **SDK layer** — `PayPalService` gained the `SubscriptionsController` methods: `createBillingPlan`, `activate/deactivateBillingPlan`, `updatePlanPricing` (pricing schemes), `updatePlanPaymentFailureThreshold` (patch), `createSubscription` (+approval URL), `getSubscription`, `activate/suspend/cancelSubscription`, `captureSubscriptionPayment` (failed-payment retry). All reuse the retry + error-normalization helpers; `createBillingPlan`/`createSubscription` carry `paypalRequestId` idempotency keys. **Key SDK facts I confirmed via the MCP** (and surfaced as constraints): - **No product-creation endpoint** in the SDK — the merchant must pre-create a PayPal **Catalog Product** in the dashboard and supply its `productId`. - The SDK's `Subscription` type omits `status` even though PayPal returns it, so I read it defensively. **DB note:** the new entity auto-creates under the dev-server's `synchronize: true` DB — no manual migration needed for local testing (a production deployment would need a generated migration). **Self-test:** 35/35 unit tests pass (8 new: ACTIVE plan with fixed-price regular cycle, subscription create with approval-URL/status/idempotency, untyped-status read, pricing update, failure-threshold patch path, cancel-with-reason, outstanding-balance capture, error wrapping). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged at 1138. --- ## 🧪 Manual verification via Postman **One-time prerequisite (PayPal sandbox dashboard):** create a **Catalog Product** and copy its **product id** (e.g. `PROD-XXXX`) — the SDK can't create products. Restart the dev server (creates the `paypal_subscription` table via synchronize). All steps below are **Admin API** (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`) unless noted. Log in first and reuse its `vendure-auth-token` as Bearer: ```graphql mutation { login(username:"superadmin", password:"superadmin"){ ... on CurrentUser { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } ``` **Step 1 — Create + activate a billing plan** ```graphql mutation { createPayPalBillingPlan(input: { productId: "PROD-XXXX", name: "Monthly Box", amount: 999, currencyCode: "USD", intervalUnit: MONTH, intervalCount: 1, totalCycles: 0, paymentFailureThreshold: 2, activateImmediately: true }) { planId status } } ``` ✅ Returns `{ planId: "P-...", status: "ACTIVE" }`. (If you set `activateImmediately: false`, then call `activatePayPalBillingPlan(planId: "P-...")` → `true`.) **Step 2 — Customer subscribes (Shop API)** — `POST http://localhost:3000/shop-api`. Register/log in a customer first (so the subscription links to them), reusing the shop `vendure-auth-token` as Bearer: ```graphql mutation { createPayPalSubscription(planId: "P-...") { id paypalSubscriptionId status approvalUrl } } ``` ✅ Returns the local subscription with `status: "APPROVAL_PENDING"` and an `approvalUrl`. **Step 3 — Approve in the browser** — open the `approvalUrl`, log in as the **sandbox buyer**, and approve the recurring payment. PayPal redirects to your return URL. **Step 4 — Sync status (Admin)** — after approval, reconcile the local mirror (use the local `id` from Step 2): ```graphql mutation { syncPayPalSubscription(id: "1") { id status lastSyncedAt } } ``` ✅ Expected `status: "ACTIVE"`. **Step 5 — View subscriptions (Admin)** ```graphql query { payPalSubscriptions(take: 25) { totalItems items { id paypalSubscriptionId planId status customerId } } } ``` ✅ The active subscription is listed. **Step 6 — Management:** - Update price: `mutation { updatePayPalBillingPlanPricing(planId:"P-...", amount:1299, currencyCode:"USD") }` → `true`. - Update failure threshold: `mutation { updatePayPalBillingPlanFailureThreshold(planId:"P-...", threshold:3) }` → `true`. - Retry a failed payment: `mutation { retryPayPalSubscriptionPayment(id:"1", amount:999, currencyCode:"USD", note:"Retry") { id status } }`. - Suspend / reactivate: `suspendPayPalSubscription(id:"1", reason:"…")` / `activatePayPalSubscription(id:"1", reason:"…")`. **Step 7 — Cancel:** - Customer (Shop API, must own it): `mutation { cancelPayPalSubscription(id:"1", reason:"No longer needed") { id status } }`. - Or merchant (Admin API): same mutation name on admin-api. ✅ `status: "CANCELLED"`; the PayPal sandbox dashboard shows the subscription cancelled. > The hourly `paypal-subscription-sync` scheduled task keeps the local statuses current automatically; Steps 4 just lets you verify immediately without waiting. --- ⏸️ **Stopping per the usecase protocol.** I won't start UC7 (Transaction Reporting) until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** --- ## References ### Endpoints - ## ✅ Fixed — sync now reflects the real PayPal status **Root cause:** The SDK's `Subscription` model doesn't declare a `status` field, and the APIMatic-generated deserializer **drops undeclared fields** from the typed `response.result`. So `result.status` was always `undefined`. My `getSubscription` then returned `'UNKNOWN'`, which `normalizeStatus()` mapped to the `'APPROVAL_PENDING'` fallback — regardless of the subscription's true state. That's why `I-5APL07TU46N4` stayed `APPROVAL_PENDING` even though PayPal showed `ACTIVE`. **The fix** (`paypal.service.ts`): `getSubscription` and `createSubscription` now read `status` from the **raw response body** (`response.body`, the full JSON PayPal returned), falling back to the typed `result.status` only if the body isn't parseable. Both methods now keep the full `ApiResponse` rather than just `.result`. **Self-test:** 36/36 unit tests pass, including a new regression test that mimics the real SDK behavior (`status` absent from `result`, present in `body`) and asserts `ACTIVE` is returned — plus a fallback test. Type-check clean; baseline unchanged. --- ## 🧪 Re-verify No restart needed for code-only changes if you're running `ts-node` with watch; otherwise restart the dev server. Then re-run sync for the already-active subscription: ```graphql mutation { syncPayPalSubscription(id: "<local id>") { id paypalSubscriptionId status lastSyncedAt } } ``` ✅ Expected now: `status: "ACTIVE"` (and `lastSyncedAt` updated). The hourly background sync task will likewise now record correct statuses. > Note: this same body-parsing path now also powers the create-subscription status and the scheduled reconciliation, so suspended/cancelled/expired states reported by PayPal will be mirrored correctly too. --- ⏸️ Still paused on the usecase protocol — reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** for UC7 (Transaction Reporting) when ready.

🤖 Claude
🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "old_string": " private toIntervalUnit(unit: PayPalIntervalUnit): IntervalUnit {", "new_string": " // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n // Transaction reporting (Use Case 7)\n // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n /**\n * @description\n * Searches PayPal account activity within a date range. PayPal limits a\n * single query to a 31-day range, so longer ranges are transparently split\n * into consecutive windows and paginated, then stitched into one report.\n *\n * Note: executed transactions can take up to ~3 hours to appear, so this is\n * intended for reconciliation, not real-time confirmation.\n *\n * @param startDateIso Inclusive range start (RFC 3339 / ISO-8601).\n * @param endDateIso Inclusive range end (RFC 3339 / ISO-8601).\n */\n async searchTransactions(\n startDateIso: string,\n endDateIso: string,\n ): Promise<PayPalTransactionReport> {\n const start = new Date(startDateIso);\n const end = new Date(endDateIso);\n if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime())) {\n throw new Error('Invalid startDate or endDate');\n }\n if (start.getTime() >= end.getTime()) {\n throw new Error('startDate must be before endDate');\n }\n\n const transactions: PayPalTransactionSummary[] = [];\n let lastRefreshedAt: string | undefined;\n try {\n for (const window of splitIntoWindows(start, end, MAX_TX_RANGE_DAYS)) {\n let page = 1;\n let totalPages = 1;\n do {\n const currentPage = page;\n const result = await this.withRetry('search transactions', async () =>\n (\n await this.transactionSearchController.searchTransactions({\n startDate: window.start,\n endDate: window.end,\n fields: 'transaction_info',\n balanceAffectingRecordsOnly: 'N',\n pageSize: TX_PAGE_SIZE,\n page: currentPage,\n })\n ).result,\n );\n totalPages = result?.totalPages ?? 1;\n lastRefreshedAt = result?.lastRefreshedDatetime ?? lastRefreshedAt;\n for (const detail of result?.transactionDetails ?? []) {\n const info = detail.transactionInfo;\n if (!info?.transactionId) {\n continue;\n }\n transactions.push({\n transactionId: info.transactionId,\n status: info.transactionStatus,\n eventCode: info.transactionEventCode,\n initiationDate: info.transactionInitiationDate,\n updatedDate: info.transactionUpdatedDate,\n currencyCode: info.transactionAmount?.currencyCode,\n value: info.transactionAmount?.value,\n feeCurrencyCode: info.feeAmount?.currencyCode,\n feeValue: info.feeAmount?.value,\n });\n }\n page++;\n if (page > MAX_TX_PAGES_PER_WINDOW) {\n Logger.warn(\n `Transaction report truncated at ${MAX_TX_PAGES_PER_WINDOW} pages for ` +\n `window ${window.start}..${window.end}`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n break;\n }\n } while (page <= totalPages);\n }\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('search transactions', e);\n }\n\n return {\n startDate: startDateIso,\n endDate: endDateIso,\n totalItems: transactions.length,\n lastRefreshedAt,\n transactions,\n };\n }\n\n /**\n * @description\n * Fetches the PayPal account balances. Balances are subject to the same\n * ~3-hour reporting delay as transactions.\n */\n async getBalances(asOfTime?: string, currencyCode?: string): Promise<PayPalBalancesReport> {\n let result: Awaited<ReturnType<TransactionSearchController['searchBalances']>>['result'];\n try {\n result = await this.withRetry('fetch balances', async () =>\n (await this.transactionSearchController.searchBalances({ asOfTime, currencyCode }))\n .result,\n );\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('fetch balances', e);\n }\n return {\n accountId: result?.accountId,\n asOfTime: result?.asOfTime,\n lastRefreshTime: result?.lastRefreshTime,\n balances: (result?.balances ?? []).map(b => ({\n currency: b.currency,\n primary: b.primary ?? false,\n totalCurrencyCode: b.totalBalance?.currencyCode,\n totalValue: b.totalBalance?.value,\n availableCurrencyCode: b.availableBalance?.currencyCode,\n availableValue: b.availableBalance?.value,\n withheldCurrencyCode: b.withheldBalance?.currencyCode,\n withheldValue: b.withheldBalance?.value,\n })),\n };\n }\n\n private toIntervalUnit(unit: PayPalIntervalUnit): IntervalUnit {" }

Add the reporting constants and the `splitIntoWindows` helper:
🤖 Claude
🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "old_string": "function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {\n return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));\n}", "new_string": "function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {\n return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));\n}\n\n/** PayPal's maximum supported transaction-search range per query. */\nconst MAX_TX_RANGE_DAYS = 31;\n/** Page size for transaction search (PayPal allows up to 500). */\nconst TX_PAGE_SIZE = 500;\n/** Safety cap on pages fetched per window to bound very large reports. */\nconst MAX_TX_PAGES_PER_WINDOW = 100;\n\n/**\n * Splits an inclusive [start, end] range into consecutive, non-overlapping\n * windows of at most `maxDays` days each, returned as RFC 3339 strings.\n */\nfunction splitIntoWindows(\n start: Date,\n end: Date,\n maxDays: number,\n): Array<{ start: string; end: string }> {\n const windows: Array<{ start: string; end: string }> = [];\n const maxMs = maxDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n let cursor = start.getTime();\n const endMs = end.getTime();\n while (cursor < endMs) {\n const windowEnd = Math.min(cursor + maxMs, endMs);\n windows.push({\n start: new Date(cursor).toISOString(),\n end: new Date(windowEnd).toISOString(),\n });\n cursor = windowEnd;\n }\n return windows;\n}" }

Baseline unchanged (1138, all pre-existing). UC7 is complete and self-tested. ## ✅ Usecase 7 (Transaction Reporting) is implemented and self-tested. A read-only Admin-API reporting module — no entities, data fetched live from PayPal, exactly as the architecture specified. **New module** (`example-plugins/paypal-plugin/reporting/`): | File | Responsibility | |------|----------------| | `reporting-types.ts` | `PayPalTransactionSummary`/`PayPalTransactionReport` and `PayPalBalance`/`PayPalBalancesReport` result types. | | `api/reporting-api-extensions.ts` | Admin SDL: `payPalTransactions(startDate, endDate)` and `payPalBalances(asOfTime, currencyCode)` queries. | | `api/paypal-reporting-admin.resolver.ts` | Resolver gated by `ReadPaymentMethod`; normalizes the `DateTime` args to ISO. | **SDK layer** — `PayPalService` gained `TransactionSearchController` plus: - `searchTransactions(startIso, endIso)` — validates the range, **automatically splits ranges > 31 days into consecutive windows** (PayPal's per-query limit) and **paginates each window** (pageSize 500, capped at 100 pages/window with a log if truncated), then stitches everything into one normalized report. Reuses the retry/error helpers. - `getBalances(asOfTime?, currencyCode?)` — maps PayPal balances (total/available/withheld per currency). **Plan constraints honored:** the 31-day max range is handled by transparent window-splitting + stitching; the ~3h reporting delay is surfaced via `lastRefreshedAt` and documented in the SDL as "reconciliation, not real-time confirmation." **Self-test:** 43/43 unit tests pass (8 new: single-window normalization, in-window pagination, 40-day range → 2 windows with correct boundaries, invalid-range rejection, error wrapping, balance mapping, arg pass-through). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged at 1138. --- ## 🧪 Manual verification via Postman These are **Admin API** queries (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`). Restart the dev server, then log in and reuse the `vendure-auth-token` as Bearer: ```graphql mutation { login(username:"superadmin", password:"superadmin"){ ... on CurrentUser { id } ... on ErrorResult { message } } } ``` **Transactions (date range)** — use a range covering your earlier sandbox test payments (remember the ~3h delay, so very recent transactions may not appear yet): ```graphql query { payPalTransactions(startDate: "2026-05-15T00:00:00Z", endDate: "2026-06-10T23:59:59Z") { startDate endDate totalItems lastRefreshedAt transactions { transactionId status eventCode initiationDate currencyCode value feeCurrencyCode feeValue } } } ``` ✅ Expected: a `PayPalTransactionReport` listing your sandbox transactions (status `S` = success, `V` = reversed/refunded, `P` = pending, `D` = denied), with amounts and fees. To exercise the **stitching**, pass a range > 31 days (e.g. 60 days) — it still returns a single combined list (the plugin makes multiple PayPal calls under the hood). **Balances:** ```graphql query { payPalBalances { accountId asOfTime lastRefreshTime balances { currency primary totalValue totalCurrencyCode availableValue withheldValue } } } ``` ✅ Expected: your sandbox business account's balances per currency (`primary: true` for the primary currency). > If a brand-new sandbox account returns an empty transaction list or empty balances, that's the ~3-hour reporting delay (and balances only populate once the account has settled activity) — not a code issue. An invalid range (start ≥ end) returns a clear `startDate must be before endDate` error. --- ⏸️ **Stopping per the usecase protocol.** UC8 (Order Shipment Tracking) is the last one — I won't start it until you reply **"Okay, proceed to the next usecase."** --- ## References ### Endpoints - 🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\paypal.service.ts", "old_string": " // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n // Transaction reporting (Use Case 7)\n // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------", "new_string": " // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n // Shipment tracking (Use Case 8)\n // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n /**\n * @description\n * Attaches shipment tracking (carrier + tracking number) to a captured\n * PayPal order so the buyer can see it in their PayPal account.\n *\n * @param paypalOrderId The PayPal order id (from the settled payment metadata).\n * @param captureId The PayPal capture id the shipment relates to.\n * @param options Tracking number, the Vendure shipping method (mapped to a\n * PayPal carrier), and whether to email the payer.\n */\n async addOrderTracking(\n paypalOrderId: string,\n captureId: string,\n options: { trackingNumber?: string; carrierMethod?: string; notifyPayer?: boolean },\n ): Promise<void> {\n const { carrier, carrierNameOther } = this.resolveCarrier(options.carrierMethod);\n try {\n await this.withRetry('add tracking to the PayPal order', async () => {\n await this.ordersController.createOrderTracking({\n id: paypalOrderId,\n body: {\n captureId,\n trackingNumber: options.trackingNumber || undefined,\n carrier,\n ...(carrierNameOther ? { carrierNameOther } : {}),\n notifyPayer: options.notifyPayer ?? true,\n },\n });\n });\n } catch (e) {\n throw this.toError('add tracking to the PayPal order', e);\n }\n }\n\n /**\n * Maps a free-text Vendure shipping-method name to a PayPal {@link ShipmentCarrier}.\n * Falls back to `OTHER` with the original name when no known carrier matches.\n * Note: the SDK enum omits `OTHER`, but the API accepts it, hence the cast.\n */\n private resolveCarrier(method?: string): {\n carrier: ShipmentCarrier;\n carrierNameOther?: string;\n } {\n const other = 'OTHER' as ShipmentCarrier;\n const trimmed = method?.trim();\n if (trimmed) {\n const candidate = trimmed.toUpperCase().replace(/\\s+/g, '_');\n if ((Object.values(ShipmentCarrier) as string[]).includes(candidate)) {\n return { carrier: candidate as ShipmentCarrier };\n }\n return { carrier: other, carrierNameOther: trimmed };\n }\n return { carrier: other, carrierNameOther: 'Other' };\n }\n\n // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n // Transaction reporting (Use Case 7)\n // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "D:\\APIMatic\\Vendure (Opus 4.8)\\packages\\dev-server\\example-plugins\\paypal-plugin\\fulfillment\\paypal-fulfillment.service.ts", "content": "import { Injectable, OnApplicationBootstrap, OnModuleDestroy } from '@nestjs/common';\nimport {\n EventBus,\n FulfillmentLine,\n FulfillmentStateTransitionEvent,\n ID,\n Logger,\n Order,\n OrderService,\n Payment,\n RequestContext,\n TransactionalConnection,\n} from '@vendure/core';\nimport { Subscription } from 'rxjs';\n\nimport {\n loggerCtx,\n PAYPAL_AUTHORIZE_PAYMENT_METHOD_CODE,\n PAYPAL_PAYMENT_METHOD_CODE,\n} from '../constants';\nimport { PayPalService } from '../paypal.service';\n\n/** The fulfillment state at which tracking is pushed to PayPal. */\nconst TRACKED_STATE = 'Shipped';\n\nconst PAYPAL_METHOD_CODES = [PAYPAL_PAYMENT_METHOD_CODE, PAYPAL_AUTHORIZE_PAYMENT_METHOD_CODE];\n\ninterface PayPalPaymentMetadata {\n paypalOrderId?: string;\n captureId?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * @description\n * Listens for fulfillment state transitions and, when a fulfillment is shipped,\n * pushes the carrier + tracking number to PayPal for each related order paid via\n * PayPal (Use Case 8). Failures are logged and never interrupt the fulfillment\n * flow.\n */\n@Injectable()\nexport class PayPalFulfillmentService implements OnApplicationBootstrap, OnModuleDestroy {\n private subscription?: Subscription;\n\n constructor(\n private readonly eventBus: EventBus,\n private readonly connection: TransactionalConnection,\n private readonly orderService: OrderService,\n private readonly payPalService: PayPalService,\n ) {}\n\n onApplicationBootstrap(): void {\n this.subscription = this.eventBus\n .ofType(FulfillmentStateTransitionEvent)\n .subscribe(event => {\n if (event.toState === TRACKED_STATE) {\n void this.pushTracking(event).catch(e => {\n const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);\n Logger.error(`Failed to push PayPal tracking: ${message}`, loggerCtx);\n });\n }\n });\n }\n\n onModuleDestroy(): void {\n this.subscription?.unsubscribe();\n }\n\n private async pushTracking(event: FulfillmentStateTransitionEvent): Promise<void> {\n const { ctx, fulfillment } = event;\n const orders = await this.getOrdersForFulfillment(ctx, fulfillment.id);\n\n for (const order of orders) {\n const payment = await this.findPayPalPayment(ctx, order.id);\n if (!payment) {\n continue;\n }\n const { paypalOrderId, captureId } = payment.metadata as PayPalPaymentMetadata;\n if (!paypalOrderId || !captureId) {\n Logger.warn(\n `Order ${order.code} PayPal payment is missing paypalOrderId/captureId; skipping tracking`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n continue;\n }\n try {\n await this.payPalService.addOrderTracking(paypalOrderId, captureId, {\n trackingNumber: fulfillment.trackingCode || undefined,\n carrierMethod: fulfillment.method,\n notifyPayer: true,\n });\n Logger.info(\n `Pushed shipment tracking to PayPal for order ${order.code} ` +\n `(capture ${captureId}, tracking \"${fulfillment.trackingCode}\")`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n } catch (e) {\n const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);\n Logger.error(\n `Failed to push tracking for order ${order.code}: ${message}`,\n loggerCtx,\n );\n }\n }\n }\n\n private async getOrdersForFulfillment(\n ctx: RequestContext,\n fulfillmentId: ID,\n ): Promise<Order[]> {\n const lines = await this.connection.getRepository(ctx, FulfillmentLine).find({\n where: { fulfillment: { id: fulfillmentId } },\n relations: ['orderLine', 'orderLine.order'],\n });\n const byId = new Map<ID, Order>();\n for (const line of lines) {\n const order = line.orderLine?.order;\n if (order) {\n byId.set(order.id, order);\n }\n }\n return Array.from(byId.values());\n }\n\n private async findPayPalPayment(\n ctx: RequestContext,\n orderId: ID,\n ): Promise<Payment | undefined> {\n const payments = await this.orderService.getOrderPayments(ctx, orderId);\n return payments.find(\n p =>\n PAYPAL_METHOD_CODES.includes(p.method) &&\n p.state === 'Settled' &&\n !!(p.metadata as PayPalPaymentMetadata)?.captureId,\n );\n }\n}\n" }

carrier: 'OTHER',\n carrierNameOther: 'Standard Shipping',\n notifyPayer: true,\n });\n });\n\n it('wraps tracking SDK errors with a safe message', async () => {\n createOrderTrackingMock.mockRejectedValue(new Error('order not found'));\n await expect(\n createService().addOrderTracking('O-1', 'CAP-1', { carrierMethod: 'UPS' }),\n ).rejects.toThrow(/Failed to add tracking to the PayPal order: order not found/);\n });\n });\n});" }

Baseline unchanged (1138, all pre-existing). UC8 is complete and self-tested — **this completes all 8 use cases of the plan.** ## ✅ Usecase 8 (Order Shipment Tracking) is implemented and self-tested. A fulfillment hook that pushes tracking to PayPal — no custom endpoints/entities, exactly as the architecture specified. **What was added:** | File | Responsibility | |------|----------------| | `fulfillment/paypal-fulfillment.service.ts` | Subscribes to `FulfillmentStateTransitionEvent`; when a fulfillment transitions to **`Shipped`**, resolves the related order(s) (via fulfillment lines → order lines → order), finds each order's settled PayPal payment, and pushes carrier + tracking. Failures are logged and never interrupt the fulfillment flow; unsubscribes on module destroy. | | `paypal.service.ts` | New `addOrderTracking(paypalOrderId, captureId, { trackingNumber, carrierMethod, notifyPayer })` → `OrdersController.createOrderTracking`, with retry/error wrapping and carrier mapping. | | `paypal.plugin.ts` | Registers `PayPalFulfillmentService` as a provider. | **Carrier handling:** I discovered the SDK's `ShipmentCarrier` enum (1412 values) has **no `OTHER` member** — though the PayPal API accepts `"OTHER"` + `carrierNameOther` (the MCP `ask` had referenced a non-existent `ShipmentCarrier.OTHER`). So `resolveCarrier` maps the Vendure shipping-method name to a known carrier when it matches (e.g. `"UPS"` → `UPS`) and otherwise sends `"OTHER"` with the method as `carrierNameOther`. **Self-test:** 46/46 unit tests pass (3 new: known-carrier mapping, unknown→OTHER+carrierNameOther, error wrapping). Type-check clean; baseline unchanged at 1138. --- ## 🧪 Manual verification via Postman Tracking is pushed **automatically** when a paid PayPal order's fulfillment is marked Shipped — no direct mutation. Restart the dev server, then: **Steps 1–5 — get a settled PayPal order** (UC1 immediate-capture): add item → `createPayPalOrder` → approve in browser → setCustomer/shipping/transition → `addPaymentToOrder(method:"paypal", metadata:{paypalOrderId})` → `PaymentSettled`. **Note the order `id`.** **Step 6 — Admin: create a fulfillment with tracking** (`POST http://localhost:3000/admin-api`, logged in as superadmin). First get the order's line id, then fulfill: ```graphql query { order(id: "<order id>") { id lines { id quantity } } } ``` ```graphql mutation { addFulfillmentToOrder(input: { handlerCode: "manual-fulfillment", arguments: [{ name: "method", value: "UPS" }, { name: "trackingCode", value: "1Z999AA10123456784" }], lines: [{ orderLineId: "<line id>", quantity: 1 }] }) { ... on Fulfillment { id state method trackingCode } ... on ErrorResult { errorCode message } } } ``` **Step 7 — Transition the fulfillment to `Shipped`** (this fires the hook): ```graphql mutation { transitionFulfillmentToState(id: "<fulfillment id>", state: "Shipped") { ... on Fulfillment { id state } ... on FulfillmentStateTransitionError { errorCode message transitionError } } } ``` ✅ Expected: the server log shows `Pushed shipment tracking to PayPal for order <code> (capture <id>, tracking "1Z999AA10123456784")`. In the **PayPal sandbox dashboard**, the captured transaction now shows the tracking number/carrier (and the buyer is emailed since `notifyPayer: true`). Because the method was `"UPS"`, it maps to PayPal's `UPS` carrier; a free-text method like `"Standard Shipping"` would be sent as carrier `OTHER` with that name. > The push is best-effort: if PayPal rejects it (e.g. capture not yet visible), the error is logged but the fulfillment still transitions normally — tracking is non-critical to order processing. --- ## 🎉 All 8 use cases complete UC1 Standard Checkout · UC2 Authorize-then-Capture · UC3 Void · UC4 Full Refund · UC5 Partial Refund · UC6 Subscriptions · UC7 Transaction Reporting · UC8 Shipment Tracking — each implemented through the `acp-paypal-server-sdk-ts` MCP server, self-tested (46 unit tests, type-check clean), and verified usecase-by-usecase. The integration also gained resilience hardening along the way (transient-retry + idempotency, the subscription-status body-parsing fix).
